***limoen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:limoen.html>limoen</a> (17822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:limoen.html>limoen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">limon</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:limoen.html>limoen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:limoenen.html>limoenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:limoen.html>limoentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lime (a green citrus fruit)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lemmet.html>lemmetje</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lime (green color)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">limoengroen</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lind.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a> (56857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>linde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lindō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>linde</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>Linde</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">lëndë</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wood, timber, material</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lind.html>lind</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:linds.html>linds</a></b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>linde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:linda.html>linda</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lindijō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>linde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linden.html>linden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lindes.html>lindes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linde.html>lindetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:linden.html>linden</a>, tree of the genus <i>Tilia</i></li></ol>

***ling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a> (15794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lings</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various marine food fish, of the genus <i>Molva</i>, resembling the cod.</li>
<li>The common <a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a>, <i>Molva molva</i>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lings</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various varieties of <a href = vnd.unilang:heather.html>heather</a> or broom.
<ol><li>Common <a href = vnd.unilang:heather.html>heather</a> (<i>Calluna <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i>)</li></ol></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">linguistics</i></span></span>.</li></ol>

***links.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a> (1061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lincs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">left, clumsy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">link</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>on the left
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>Zie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you see the car <b>on the left</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to the left
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volgende.html>volgende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkeerslicht.html>verkeerslicht</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:afslaan.html>afslaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Turn <b>left</b> at the next traffic light.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re going to the <b>left</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>When used as a modifier, before a noun, the form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linker.html>linker</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the adverb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>linkser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">linkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">not comparable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> left
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlek.html>vlek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>linkse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoen.html>schoen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There’s a spot on your <b>left</b> shoe.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>linkse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>ideeën</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Those are <b>left-wing</b> ideas.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrijven.html>schrijven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’m <b>left-handed</b>, you cannot write with my <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>The left, the left side or tendency, especially in politics and any ideology.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opinie.html>opinie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That’s an opinion that could have come from the <b>left</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">link</i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***linnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:linnen.html>linnen</a> (19376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">linijn</i>, originally an adjective. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linnen.html>linnen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linnen.html>linnens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linnen.html>linnentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Linen, a cloth made from flax.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lijnwaad</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something made of linen.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lijnwaad</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linnen.html>linnen</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Made of linen.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></span></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:landbouw.html>landbouw</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:kleding.html>kleding</a>)</span> product <a href = vnd.unilang:afkomstig.html>afkomstig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlas.html>vlas</a></li>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>Heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:linnen.html>linnen</a></b>?</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lint.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lint.html>lint</a> (5593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Of uncertain origin. Probably a shortening of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijnen.html>lijnde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">line</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></i>). Alternatively from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">linteum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lint.html>lint</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linten.html>linten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lintje.html>lintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A ribbon, a cloth <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> or non-textile (non-adhesive) tape.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A decoration, a medal, especially in chivalric, civil and military contexts.</li></ol>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lintworm.html>lintworm</a> (18773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lint.html>lint</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ribbon, tape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">worm</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***linze.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:linze.html>linze</a> (81786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lins.html>lins</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lynsen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">linse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">linsa</i>, likely a borrowing from an unidentified source.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lēns</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">lęšis</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">лѧща</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lęšta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> sounding too similar for a coincidence, however different enough to prohibit reconstruction of a common PIE protoform.
</p><p>If ultimately a Non-IE loanword, locating the source <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> virtually impossible because cultivation of lentil <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> widespread in the region since the Neolithic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linze.html>linze</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linzen.html>linzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:linze.html>linsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lentil</span>, <i>Lens culinaris</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">legume</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lentil</span>, the seed of <i>Lens culinaris</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">pulse</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = </p>
<ol><li>to read <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a>
<dl><dd>[...] <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> close up <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Wesley <a href = vnd.unilang:vlak.html>vlak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doelpunt.html>doelpunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:liplezen.html>liplazen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duidelijk.html>duidelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a> ´Robben.´</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> no, in a close up of Wesley, just after the goal, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> clearly discerned the word ´Robben´ by lip reading.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used in its infinitive form to mean lip reading and hence uses the definite article <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>. Other forms are sporadically attested.</li></ul>

***lippenstift.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>lippenstift</a> (6525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lip</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stift.html>stift</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lipstick.html>lipstick</a></i>, perhaps through <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>Lippenstift</a></i> (where only this form exists).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>lippenstift</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstiften.html>lippenstiften</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>lippenstiftje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:lipstick.html>lipstick</a></li>
<li>The material a <a href = vnd.unilang:lipstick.html>lipstick</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> made of.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lippenstift.html>lippenstift</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> — <i>She puts on her <a href = vnd.unilang:lipstick.html>lipstick</a></i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***liquideren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:liquideren.html>liquideren</a> (23117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">liquider</i>
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liquideren.html>liquideren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to liquidate</li>
<li>to root out, to clear out</li>
<li>to take out, to kill</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a> (12916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lyre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">līra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">any fleshy part of the body, muscle, calf of the <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ligwizô</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lihwizô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thigh, groin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lekʷs-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewks-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">groin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lies</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">groin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">lår</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thigh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lires.html>lires</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Flesh, brawn, or muscle; the fleshy part of a person or animal in contradistinction to the bone and skin.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The fleshy part of a roast capon, etc. as distinguished from a limb or joint.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lyre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hlýr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheeks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">plural</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lere.html>lere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hlēor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheek, countenance, complexion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lires.html>lires</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The cheek.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Face; appearance of the face or skin; complexion; hue.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">líri</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">lira</i>.
</p>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orkney" class="extiw" title="w:Orkney">Orkney</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shetland" class="extiw" title="w:Shetland">Shetland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> ornithology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Manx shearwater (bird).</li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***litanie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanie</a> (103615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">letanie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">letanīa</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">litanīa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λιτανεία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litaneía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The classical Latin and Greek forms with <i>li-</i> influenced the current Dutch spelling.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>litany <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">liturgical prayer consisting of series of prayers</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr />

***liturgie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgie</a> (74658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līturgia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λειτουργία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leitourgía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">work in public</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A liturgy, predetermined or prescribed set of (religious) rituals and associated customs, attributes etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paus.html>Paus</a> Gregorius <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> uniformizering <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:katholieke.html>Katholieke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgie</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:inclusief.html>inclusief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruik.html>gebruik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Latijnse teksen</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Pope Gregory the Great <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> a lot to uniformize the Catholic liturgy, including the obligatory use of Latin texts</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A liturgy, a booklet with <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a> about the <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a> sung and texts read in a mass or other religious service.</li>
<li>A liturgy, Ancient Greek service to the public interest</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">liturg</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">liturgiek</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">liturgisch</span></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a>)</span> eertijds <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dienst.html>dienst</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:bate.html>bate</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenschap.html>gemeenschap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waartoe.html>waartoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rijken.html>rijken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diensten.html>diensten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rituelen.html>rituelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:religieuze.html>religieuze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijeenkomsten.html>bijeenkomsten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:christenen.html>christenen</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbes</a> (81753)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbesen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">endearing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> large, well-mannered or friendly dog</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">endearing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kindly but oafish person</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only rarely used any more.</li></ul>
